SELECT CASE
    WHEN EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Material] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [Category] AS [c] ON [m].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
        WHERE [c].[CategoryName] = @__file_CtegoryName_0) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
